				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Es ist dir gesagt, Mensch, was gut ist, BWV 45 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (in 7 movements)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1726 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Es ist dir gesagt, Mensch, was gut ist
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">You have been told, O man, what is Good
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ca, es">Es ist dir gesagt</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/184706549">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Es_ist_dir_gesagt,_Mensch,_was_gut_ist,_BWV_45">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/184706549">184706549</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300007280">300007280</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb139096061">139096061</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 45&#160;; BC A113
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 132
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>E major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (in 7 movements)
<dl><dt><ul><li>Parte prima
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Chorus: Es ist dir gesagt, Mensch, was gut ist (E&#160;major)
</dd><dd>2. Recitativo (tenor): Der Höchste läßt mich seinen Willen wissen (B&#160;major-G<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span>&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>3. Aria (tenor): Weiß ich Gottes Rechte (C<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span>&#160;minor)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Parte seconda
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>4. Arioso (bass): Es werden viele zu mir sagen an jenem Tage (A&#160;major)
</dd><dd>5. Aria (alto): Wer Gott bekennt (F<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span>&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>6. Recitativo (alto): So wird denn Herz und mund (E&#160;major)
</dd><dd>7. Choral: Gib, daß ich tu mit fleiß (E&#160;major)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1726 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1726-08-11 in Leipzig
</td></tr>

<td>1863 (BGA)
</td></tr>

</th>
